<div class="post-info"><span class="date published time" title="2016-02-01T07:58:37+00:00">February 1, 2016</span>  | <span class="post-comments"><a href="http://www.gaynycdad.com/2016/02/giveaway-25-walmartsams-club-gift-card.html#comments">732 Comments</a></span> </div><div class="entry-content"><p><a href="http://www.gaynycdad.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/WalmartCard5-300.jpg"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-34899" src="http://www.gaynycdad.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/WalmartCard5-300.jpg" alt="WalmartCard5 300" width="400" height="255" /></a></p>
<p>The above is not what you will receive, your winning card will be from Sam&#8217;s Club. They are the same company and the gift cards are interchangeable between all their stores!</p>
<p><strong>G</strong><strong>IVEAWAY:</strong></p>
<p>One lucky reader of the GayNYCDad award winning blog, will receive a $25 Sam&#8217;s Club Gift Card! This works at Walmart as well, they are owned by the same family!</p>
<p>Mandatory Entries: Sign up for my blog via subscription and confirm your subscription! Leave a comment to tell that you have done so and the RSS feed does not count.</p>
<p>Extra entries:<br />
1. Follow me on twitter <a href="http://www.twitter.com/gaynycdad">www.twitter.com/gaynycdad</a> (click above right).<br />
2. Share this contest on your Facebook page using the button on the bottom of the post and share that link in your entry comment here.<br />
3. Retweet this info (you can use the tweet button at the bottom of the post) and leave me a comment with a link to your retweet.<br />
4. Retweet daily and leave a comment daily that you have done this.<br />
5. Extra entry for leaving a comment on a non-giveaway post &#8211; you must leave a comment here as well to tell me that you have done so to get the entry.<br />
6. Visit<a href="https://www.facebook.com/GayNYCDad"> my Facebook page here</a>, leave me a separate comment telling me you have done so.<br />
7. Follow me on <a href="http://www.instagram.com/gaynycdad">Instagram</a> and leave a separate comment!<br />
8. Follow me on <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/gaynycdad">Pinterest</a> and leave a separate comment!<br />
9. Follow me on <a href="https://plus.google.com/107045938060665512370/posts">Google Plus</a>! And leave a separate comment!<br />
10. Subscribe to my <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/GayNYCDad">Youtube channel</a> and leave me a comment here stating that you did!</p>
<p><strong>You must leave a separate comment in the comments field for each entry that you make to be entered!</strong> If you are already any of these things, to enter just leave a separate comment reminding me of that! Contest ends midnight, February 21, 2016. Prizes must be claimed within 48 hours. Maximum winnings of 2 giveaways per every 90 days. See <a href="http://www.gaynycdad.com/2009/11/about.html">official rules</a> for more information.</p>
<p><strong>Every entry requires a separate comment!</strong></p>
<p>Thanks and good-luck.</p>
